### Theorem `t:geom intertwiner`
- **Claim ID:** `GLC3:theorem:t:geom intertwiner`
- **Location:** `gaits3.tex` lines 2531-2536
- **Context:** The local semi-infinite category
- **Dependencies (outgoing):** 0 — _(none found by label-scan)_
- **Used by (incoming):** 1 — [`GLC3:corollary:c:geom intertwiner`](./GLC3.md#glc3-corollary-c-geom-intertwiner-ec90d400)

```tex
\label{t:geom intertwiner} The composite functor $$\Dmod(\Gr_G)^{\fL(N(P))} \hookrightarrow \Dmod(\Gr_G)\twoheadrightarrow \Dmod(\Gr_G)_{\fL(N^-_P)}$$ is an equivalence (as factorization categories).
```

- **Claim ID:** `GLC3:remark:r:semiinf restr gen`
- **Location:** `gaits3.tex` lines 4651-4658
- **Context:** Jacquet and Wakimoto functors for Kac-Moody modules
- **Dependencies (outgoing):** 2 — [`GLC3:lemma:l:wak restr to n`](./GLC3.md#glc3-lemma-l-wak-restr-to-n-52c2c15f), [`GLC3:proposition:p:wak-explicit, almost`](./GLC3.md#glc3-proposition-p-wak-explicit-almost-7981e941)
- **Used by (incoming):** 1 — [`GLC3:corollary:c:wak-explicit`](./GLC3.md#glc3-corollary-c-wak-explicit-9bd8b551)

```tex
\label{r:semiinf restr gen} A similar result holds for any parabolic $\fp_2$ in place of the Borel, or more generally, any subalgebra $\fh \subset \fg$ with the property that $\fp^-+\fh = \fg$. In particular, we can apply it to $\fh=\fn$, see \lemref{l:wak restr to n} below.
```

- **Location:** `gaits3.tex` lines 22117-22120
- **Context:** The Langlands functor is an equivalence on the Eisenstein part(s)
- **Dependencies (outgoing):** 1 — [`GLC3:proposition:p:AP 1`](./GLC3.md#glc3-proposition-p-ap-1-cdecc294)
- **Used by (incoming):** 1 — [`GLC3:remark:auto0001@L941`](./GLC3.md#glc3-remark-auto0001-l941-218591a7)

```tex
\label{l:line bundle is enough} Let $\CY$ be an algebraic stack, and let $\CA_\CY$ be a unital associative algebra object in $\QCoh(\CY)$. Assume that $\CA_\CY$ is a line bundle. Then the unit map $\CO_\CY\to \CA_\CY$ is an isomorphism.
```

---

<a id="glc3-lemma-l-gr-nakayama-00284992"></a>
### Lemma `l:gr Nakayama`
- **Claim ID:** `GLC3:lemma:l:gr Nakayama`
- **Location:** `gaits3.tex` lines 22324-22329
- **Context:** The Langlands functor is an equivalence on the Eisenstein part(s)
- **Dependencies (outgoing):** 4 — [`GLC3:corollary:c:* back and forth AG`](./GLC3.md#glc3-corollary-c-back-and-forth-ag-ea43f43b), [`GLC3:lemma:l:grading pos`](./GLC3.md#glc3-lemma-l-grading-pos-9b9ffca5), [`GLC3:proposition:p:AP 1`](./GLC3.md#glc3-proposition-p-ap-1-cdecc294), [`GLC3:proposition:p:AP 2`](./GLC3.md#glc3-proposition-p-ap-2-3d590519)
- **Used by (incoming):** 0 — _(none)_

- **Unresolved `\*ref{…}` targets (not claims):** 3

```tex
\label{l:gr Nakayama} Let $A$ be a non-negatively graded commutative algebra. Denote by $A_0$ its degree $0$ component. Let $M$ be a non-negatively graded $A$-module. Suppose that the $A_0$-module $$M_0:=A_0\underset{A}\otimes M$$ is invertible. Then $M$ is itself invertible.
```

- **Claim ID:** `GLC3:lemma:l:compact vs almost compact`
